WARNING:tensorflow:From /data/data/wlh/apps/miniconda3/envs/spider/lib/python3.6/site-packages/tensorflow/contrib/data/python/ops/batching.py:273: map_and_batch (from tensorflow.python.data.experimental.ops.batching) is deprecated and will be removed in a future version.
Instructions for updating:
